How to work a req: check internal TalentBase coverage first (every count opens to real candidate records in the app), then run Net 1 → Net 2 → Net 3 in LinkedIn Recruiter using the copy buttons, then send the InMail sequence (initial → day 3-4 → day 7-8 → day 12-14 close). Every message asks for interest, a current resume, and availability. Limited-confidence = no JD on file (105 of 129) — confirm scope with the HM before spending InMail credits. Merge fields {FIRST} and {COMPANY} personalize per candidate.

Algorithms / AI Engineering (Merrimack NH)

1 requisition · 1490
▶
Principal algorithm and AI engineering for defense sensing and autonomy — where models meet fielded hardware.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 30-100 profiles
Title
("Algorithm Engineer" OR "AI Engineer" OR "Machine Learning Engineer" OR "Research Scientist" OR "Perception Engineer") AND (Principal OR Staff OR Senior OR Lead)
Keywords
(algorithm OR "machine learning" OR "computer vision" OR perception OR "sensor fusion" OR tracking OR "signal processing") AND (C++ OR Python OR MATLAB) AND (defense OR aerospace OR radar OR EO/IR OR autonomy)
Filters: Location: New England + national (pool is national). Years: 10+. Industry: Defense & Space, Research.
Run notes: Elite pool — every profile is a named target.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 200-500 profiles
Title
("Machine Learning" OR "Computer Vision" OR "Algorithm" OR "Perception" OR "Autonomy")
Keywords
(deep learning OR CNN OR tracking OR estimation OR Kalman OR "signal processing" OR embedded ML) AND (deploy OR production OR "real-time" OR edge)
Filters: Location: United States. Years: 7+. Target defense-AI companies + labs.
Run notes: Raid net — defense-AI startups + FFRDC staff.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 800+ profiles
Title
("Machine Learning Engineer" OR "AI" OR "Data Scientist" OR "Research Engineer")
Keywords
("computer vision" OR perception OR "sensor" OR "signal processing") AND (PhD OR MS OR research)
Filters: Location: United States + top-program alumni (MIT, CMU, Stanford, Georgia Tech). Years: 5+.
Run notes: Discovery net; screen for real-time/edge deployment (not notebook-only).

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: MIT Lincoln LaboratoryDraperSTR (Woburn MA)Charles River Analytics (Cambridge)RTX BBN (Cambridge)AndurilShield AI
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: Palantir (defense)Scale AI (federal)Raytheon / Lockheed AI orgsMITREKitwareAretéSystems & Technology Research
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: autonomy startups (Skydio, Zipline alumni)MIT/CMU robotics lab alumniquant researchers seeking mission (occasionally convert)

Exclusions

Exclude notebook-only data scientists without deployment record; exclude non-US-persons (ITAR); exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already on req 1490.

InMail Sequence (family template — per-req personalized versions inside each req below)

Subjects: Models that ship on aircraft | Edge AI, consequences included | Your research instincts, fielded
Initial InMail
{FIRST} — the gap between models that demo and models that deploy is where most AI careers stall, and your record of shipping is why I'm writing. The search is retained — a {ROLE} in {LOC} with Elbit Systems of America: principal-level algorithms for defense sensing — tracking, fusion, real-time inference where 'production' means airborne hardware with SWaP limits and lives in the loop. {TECHLINE} You were mapped into this search for deployment evidence plus mathematical depth; the field is full of one without the other, and this seat requires both. What I'll only describe live is the sensor programs this work feeds and the runway behind them — researchers find that part persuasive. If constraints make problems interesting to you rather than smaller, send a current resume and a pair of windows that genuinely fit. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — mission, stated plainly: the models here extend human perception for people in danger. Few applied-AI seats can write that sentence honestly. The conversation offer stands.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — the technical honesty: latency budgets in milliseconds, compute in watts, adversarial conditions by definition, and validation standards that make MLOps look leisurely. The hard version of the problem — which is the point. Worth a call?
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — I'll close here; this community is small and I'd rather be remembered as respectful. A resume on file means first word when the next principal algorithms seat opens. Good work matters — yours included.
Verify on first call: Verify deployment record (what hardware, what latency), US-person status, and depth vs breadth (principal seat needs depth).
Flexibility: HM open to radar/RF signal-processing depth in lieu of EO/IR; C++ deployment fluency is the constant.

Configuration Management (Fort Worth TX · Detroit MI · Merrimack NH)

2 requisitions · 1524, 1525
▶
Configuration and data management for defense programs — baselines, change control and product structure that keep fielded configurations honest.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 20-80 per site
Title
("Configuration Analyst" OR "Configuration Management" OR "CM Analyst" OR "Configuration Specialist") AND (I OR II OR Senior OR Sr)
Keywords
("configuration management" OR "change control" OR CCB OR baseline OR "EIA-649" OR ECO OR ECN) AND (defense OR aerospace OR engineering OR manufacturing) AND (Windchill OR Teamcenter OR PLM OR Agile PLM OR SAP)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (DFW 40 mi / Detroit 40 mi / Merrimack 30 mi) — multi-site req: run all three in parallel. Years: I: 0-3, Senior: 5+. Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace.
Run notes: Small discipline; PLM-tool fluency is the strongest marker.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 100-300 per site
Title
("Configuration" OR "Document Control" OR "Data Management" OR "PLM Analyst" OR "Change Analyst")
Keywords
("change control" OR "engineering change" OR baseline OR "bill of material" OR BOM OR "document control" OR release management) AND (engineering OR product OR manufacturing)
Filters: Location: 50 mi per site. Years: per level. Auto-industry PLM/BOM analysts (Detroit) convert directly.
Run notes: Document-control and PLM analysts step up into CM cleanly — screen for change-process ownership.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 300+ profiles
Title
(Configuration OR "Document Control" OR PLM)
Keywords
(engineering OR manufacturing OR aerospace OR automotive) AND (change OR baseline OR release)
Filters: Location: state-wide per site + remote-flag profiles. Years: any for Level I.
Run notes: Pipeline net for Level I — detail-oriented admins with PLM exposure trainable.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin (Fort Worth)BellGeneral Dynamics Land Systems (Sterling Heights)BAE SystemsRaytheonL3HarrisLeonardo DRS
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: Ford / GM / Stellantis PLM & release analysts (Detroit)Bosch / ZF / Magna (Detroit suppliers)Collins AerospaceTriumph GroupElbit peers' CM orgs
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: document-control specialists in regulated mfgTeamcenter/Windchill administratorsmilitary logistics/supply specialists (92A) transitioning

Exclusions

Exclude software-release-only 'configuration' profiles (build engineers) unless PLM evidence exists; exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already assigned in TalentBase.

InMail Sequence (family template — per-req personalized versions inside each req below)

Subjects: Be the source of truth | Baselines that match the field | Change control with a spine
Initial InMail
{FIRST} — configuration management done seriously is a source-of-truth profession, and your background suggests you practice it that way. Elbit Systems of America is staffing a {ROLE} in {LOC}: real change control on defense product baselines — CCBs with authority, PLM discipline, and configurations that must match what is physically fielded, because auditors and operators both check. {TECHLINE} You were contacted for evidence of owned change process — ECOs run, boards supported, baselines defended — which is rarer than the title suggests. Defense CM is also a quietly excellent career: EIA-649 fluency and audit-ready judgment appreciate every year. The program this protects is the part worth hearing live. If being the person everyone trusts to know what's true sounds like your work, send a current resume and two calm windows on your calendar. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — mission, in CM terms: when the fielded unit matches the baseline, the person using it can trust every part in their hands. That's what the discipline protects. Glad to expand.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — the craft texture: multi-site change coordination, PLM data that has to be right, and the satisfying authority of a well-run board. Detail-minded people build durable careers on exactly this. Worth a short call?
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — closing tidily, as befits the discipline. One resume on file means first call on the next CM seat. If you know a change-control natural, I'd welcome the introduction — and return it.
Verify on first call: Verify hands-on change-process ownership (ECOs run, boards supported), PLM tool depth, and multi-site coordination comfort.
Flexibility: Level I trainable from document control; Senior requires owned CCB/baseline record.

What I'll share live is the growth arc inside this security organization — and why joining early matters. If defending consequential things appeals more than patching indifferent ones, fire over a current resume and two windows. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America

Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — the technical reality: cleared environments, modern tooling, real incident tempo, and RMF work that builds career capital most security resumes never touch. Every year here compounds. Worth a look while the team is still forming.
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — closing this thread without ceremony. Cleared-security seats recur as this bench grows; a resume on file puts you at the top of that call list. A quiet pointer to a sharp cleared engineer works just as well — I repay both.
Verify on first call: Verify US citizenship/clearance eligibility first; hands-on vs paper-compliance balance per req; for Cloud Engineer verify IaC depth.
Flexibility: Req 1277 is remote-eligible — use it to win candidates the DFW reqs cannot; finance/healthcare security converts with citizenship.

The current design surface includes NASDAQ, ESLT and TASE — architecture questions welcome on the call. Your selection wasn't algorithmic: circuit depth, qualification exposure and evidence of end-to-end ownership are the three filters, and you cleared all of them. The program specifics — and the reason this seat opened — are better delivered in conversation. If owning hardware from schematic to field support is the job you've been describing to yourself, reply with a current resume and two open windows. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1
{FIRST} — why it matters, without varnish: these boxes end up in aircraft protecting the people flying them. The design reviews here carry that weight comfortably. Conversation remains open.
Follow-up 2
{FIRST} — the engineering texture: mixed-signal margins that have to survive temperature and vibration, power trees with no forgiveness, EMC that's designed in rather than patched on. Peers who review like they mean it. If that's your standard, let's compare notes.
Follow-up 3
{FIRST} — final touch from me, light as promised. Senior EE seats in this corridor cross my desk regularly; being on my short list costs you one resume and nothing else. Good building, either way.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 40-150 profiles per site
Title
("Engineering Technician" OR "Electronics Technician" OR "Test Technician" OR "Engineering Technologist") AND (II OR Senior OR Staff OR Principal)
Keywords
(soldering OR "IPC-A-610" OR "J-STD" OR troubleshooting OR oscilloscope OR multimeter OR "test equipment" OR schematic) AND (electronics OR electrical OR avionics)
Filters: Location: per req (Roanoke 25 mi / DFW 30 mi) — techs do not relocate; stay local. Years: 3+ (Senior/Staff: 7+). Veteran filter ON.
Run notes: Local + veteran net is the whole game for techs.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 200-500 profiles per site
Title
("Technician" OR "Technologist") AND (electronic OR electrical OR test OR maintenance OR avionics OR calibration)
Keywords
(troubleshoot OR repair OR test OR calibration OR assembly) AND (electronics OR avionics OR radar OR communications)
Filters: Location: 40 mi per site. Add military: Navy AT/ET/FC, Army 94E/94F/35T, USAF 2A5/2A6 — search these MOS codes as keywords. Schools: ECPI, Virginia Western CC (ROA); TSTC (TX).
Run notes: Veteran MOS search is the highest-yield channel.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 500+ profiles
Title
(Technician OR Technologist OR "Field Service")
Keywords
(electronics OR electrical OR mechanical) AND (military OR veteran OR manufacturing OR lab)
Filters: Location: 60 mi per site + transitioning-military bases (Fort Barfoot VA / NAS Fort Worth JRB). Years: any.
Run notes: Pipeline net + SkillBridge/transition programs.

Human Resources & Talent Acquisition (Roanoke VA · Fort Worth TX)

6 requisitions · 1419, 1557, 1421, 1530, 1531, 1570
▶
HR generalists and talent advisors for a growing defense manufacturer — real employee populations, hard hiring targets, mission stakes.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 40-150 per site
Title
("HR Generalist" OR "Human Resources Generalist" OR "Talent Advisor" OR "Talent Acquisition" OR Recruiter) AND (II OR Senior)
Keywords
(HRBP OR "employee relations" OR onboarding OR HRIS OR Workday OR "full cycle" OR sourcing OR requisition) AND (manufacturing OR aerospace OR defense OR industrial)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (Roanoke 30 mi / DFW 40 mi). Years: 3+ (Senior: 6+). Industry: Defense, Manufacturing, Staffing & Recruiting.
Run notes: Manufacturing-HR profiles are the precision cut.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 250-600 per site
Title
("HR Generalist" OR "HR Business Partner" OR Recruiter OR "Talent Acquisition Specialist" OR "People Operations")
Keywords
("employee relations" OR recruiting OR "talent acquisition" OR HRIS OR benefits OR "performance management") AND (hourly OR manufacturing OR plant OR technical OR engineering)
Filters: Location: 50 mi per site. Years: 2+. Include agency recruiters (Aerotek, Actalent, Insight Global alumni) for Talent Advisor reqs.
Run notes: Agency-to-corporate is the classic Talent Advisor pipeline — use it.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 800+ profiles
Title
(HR OR Recruiter OR "Talent" OR "People")
Keywords
(recruiting OR "human resources" OR talent)
Filters: Location: metro-wide per site. Years: 1+.
Run notes: Volume net; screen for volume-hiring and technical-recruiting evidence.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin HR (Fort Worth)Bell HRVolvo Trucks HR (Dublin VA)Wabtec (Salem VA)BAE SystemsGeneral DynamicsBoeing
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: Aerotek / Actalent (technical recruiters)Insight GlobalAlcon (Fort Worth)American Airlines people orgCarilion Clinic HR (Roanoke)Yokohama HR (Salem)
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: SHRM-certified pool (SHRM-CP/SCP keywords)military 42A / personnel officers transitioningRPO recruiters (Cielo, Korn Ferry RPO, Sevenstep)

Exclusions

Exclude pure benefits/payroll-only profiles for generalist seats; exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already assigned in TalentBase.

InMail Sequence (family template — per-req personalized versions inside each req below)

Subjects: HR where the plant knows your name | Recruit for something worth joining | A population that builds real things
Initial InMail
{FIRST} — HR careers are made in operations that take people seriously, and that's the distinction behind this note. Elbit Systems of America needs a {ROLE} in {LOC}: a real population — engineers, technicians, production teams building defense systems — where employee relations carry weight, hiring targets have mission behind them, and HR sits inside the operation rather than beside it. {TECHLINE} Your background matched what the site leadership sketched: practical judgment, plant-floor credibility, and the spine for hard conversations. That's a selection, not a compliment. What I'd rather share by phone is how this site is growing and what that means for the HR bench joining now. If being essential — not administrative — is the version of HR you practice, send along a current resume and two easy times to reach you. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — the mission carries into HR plainly: the people you support build equipment that protects other people. Employee relations feels different with that sentence underneath it. Glad to say more.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — for the TA side of your craft: recruiting cleared and technical talent is the hardest lane in the field — and the most valuable book you can build. This seat builds it with real requisition flow. Worth a conversation.
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — final note, kept human: if timing's wrong, no explanation owed. The function here grows with headcount; a resume on file means the next seat finds you first. Referrals welcomed and returned in kind.
Verify on first call: Verify hourly/manufacturing population experience for generalist reqs; req-load and technical-pipeline evidence for Talent Advisor reqs.
Flexibility: Agency/RPO recruiters welcome for Talent Advisor seats; generalist seats prefer plant exposure.

3 requisitions · 1437, 1372, 1444
▶
Protecting cleared facilities, people and information — NISPOM-grade industrial security and executive information security for a defense manufacturer.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect AFSO: 20-60 local · CISO/Mgr: 60-200 national
Title
("Facility Security Officer" OR FSO OR AFSO OR "Personnel Security" OR "Industrial Security" OR CISO OR "Chief Information Security Officer")
Keywords
(NISPOM OR DCSA OR "32 CFR 117" OR DISS OR NBIS OR "security clearance" OR "cleared facility" OR PERSEC OR INFOSEC) AND (defense OR government OR contractor)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (Roanoke 30 mi for AFSO / DFW 40 mi + national for CISO & PERSEC Mgr). Years: AFSO 3+, Manager 8+, CISO 15+. Industry: Defense & Space.
Run notes: Cleared-security community is small and networked — precision only.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 100-300 profiles
Title
("Security Manager" OR "Security Specialist" OR "Security Officer" OR "Information Security" AND (Director OR VP OR Manager))
Keywords
(clearance OR cleared OR DoD OR federal) AND (security OR NISPOM OR CISSP OR RMF OR "insider threat")
Filters: Location: widen per seat; CISO national. Years: per seat. Include DCSA/DoD CAF alumni and military security-manager veterans.
Run notes: Government-to-industry crossover net.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 300-800 profiles
Title
("Security" AND (Officer OR Manager OR Specialist OR Director))
Keywords
(industrial OR corporate OR information) AND security
Filters: Location: per seat. Years: per seat.
Run notes: Discovery net — screen hard for cleared-environment depth.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin security orgsBellRaytheonL3HarrisBAE SystemsNorthrop GrummanGeneral Dynamics
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: DCSA alumniDoD CAF alumniLeidos / SAIC / Booz security staffNCMS (Society of Industrial Security) membersmilitary security managers (31/97 series, USAF SF)
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: financial-sector CISOs open to defense (for 1372)corporate security directors (F500)cleared-facility security staff at smaller GovCons ready to step up

Exclusions

Exclude guard-force-only profiles for FSO/PERSEC seats; exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already assigned in TalentBase.

Program Management (Fort Worth TX · Merrimack NH)

9 requisitions · 1497, 1501, 1502, 663, 810, 845, 1265, 1500, 1572
▶
Defense program management — cost, schedule and performance on funded DoD programs, from sustainment through new starts.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 50-180 profiles
Title
("Program Manager" OR "Program Scheduler" OR "Master Scheduler") AND (II OR III OR Senior OR Master)
Keywords
(EVMS OR "earned value" OR "integrated master schedule" OR IMS OR "cost account" OR CDRL OR "DoD program" OR sustainment) AND (defense OR aerospace OR government)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (DFW 40 mi / Merrimack 30 mi). Years: PM II 5+, PM III 8+. Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace.
Run notes: DFW is the deepest defense-PM market in the country outside DC.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 250-600 profiles
Title
("Program Manager" OR "Project Manager" OR "IPT Lead" OR "Program Management")
Keywords
(PMP OR EVMS OR milestone OR "cost schedule" OR risk OR stakeholder) AND (defense OR aerospace OR manufacturing OR engineering)
Filters: Location: widen 60 mi + relocation-open for PM III. Years: 5+. Include transitioning military acquisition officers (keywords: DAWIA, acquisition corps).
Run notes: Core net — military acquisition officers are an elite feeder.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 1,000+ profiles
Title
("Program Manager" OR "Project Manager")
Keywords
(program OR project) AND (hardware OR engineering OR manufacturing OR government)
Filters: Location: metro per site. Years: 4+.
Run notes: Discovery net; screen hard for hardware-program scope vs IT-project scope.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin (Fort Worth — F-35 program office alumni)BellRaytheon (McKinney)L3Harris (Greenville)General DynamicsBAE Systems (Nashua NH)Northrop Grumman
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: Textron SystemsCollins AerospaceLeonardo DRSKratosAmentum / KBR / V2X (sustainment PMs)Draper / MITRE program staff
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: military acquisition officers (DAWIA II/III) transitioningPMI chapter leadership (PMP+defense)aerospace suppliers' program offices (Triumph, Spirit)

Exclusions

Exclude IT/software-only project managers; exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already assigned in TalentBase.

InMail Sequence (family template — per-req personalized versions inside each req below)

Subjects: Run the program, not the deck | Authority and accountability, together | EVMS with actual decisions attached
Initial InMail
{FIRST} — program managers divide into those who report on programs and those who run them; everything in your record points to the running kind, and that is the entire admission standard here. I hold a retained mandate — {ROLE}, {LOC} — with Elbit Systems of America: funded defense programs with the full toolkit — an IMS you own, EVMS that's used rather than performed, CDRLs, customer counterparts who know their business — and leadership that backs the PM's call. {TECHLINE} Your selection rests on program scale and customer-facing evidence, the two credentials that don't fake well. What belongs in a conversation rather than an InMail: which portfolio this seat anchors and why it's growing. If accountable authority is the arrangement you've been looking for, send a current resume and two windows you can hold. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — the mission stakes are unusually legible in this portfolio: deliveries here equip people who are counting on the schedule you defend. PMs say that focus is clarifying. Happy to elaborate.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — the craft challenge: baselines that survive contact, risk registers that drive decisions rather than decorate reviews, and customer reviews where prepared beats polished. If that's the game you play well, we should talk.
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — final touch, professionally light. Program seats in this portfolio recur; a resume on file means the next mandate finds you pre-posting. A referral to a strong defense PM is equally welcome — and remembered.
Verify on first call: Verify program scale (TCV, team size), EVMS hands-on (not just exposure), customer-facing record; scheduler req: verify IMS build-from-scratch.
Flexibility: Military acquisition officers (DAWIA II+) map to PM II/III with translation help.

I'm retained on a {ROLE} search in {LOC} for Elbit Systems of America: enterprise quality for a growing defense manufacturer — AS9100 at scale, DCMA and customer-facing quality, multi-site harmonization, and cultural authority that makes 'stop the line' a real sentence. {TECHLINE} Your name surfaced through deliberate mapping, not a keyword sweep: multi-site scope, customer-quality exposure and a leadership record are the three requirements, and your career shows all three. If building rather than maintaining is the chapter you want next, send a current resume and two discreet windows, and I'll frame the mandate properly. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — one signal worth weighing: quality here is being invested in ahead of growth, not audited after it. Leaders tell me that's the difference they look for and rarely find. The conversation stays between us.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8

Filters: Location: Merrimack NH 25 mi. Years: 8+. Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace. Keywords add: clearance OR secret.

Systems Engineering — MTC Program (Charleston SC · Fort Worth TX · Detroit MI · Yuma AZ)

9 requisitions · 1257, 1289, 1366, 1487, 1488, 1491, 1492, 1503, 1516
▶
Systems engineering on fielded combat-vehicle and mission systems — requirements through integration, safety and test, across the program's build and proving-ground sites.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect Detroit: 80-200 · DFW: 60-150 · CHS/Yuma: 15-50
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "Systems Integration Engineer" OR "System Safety Engineer" OR "Chief Engineer" OR "Systems Engineering Manager") AND (Senior OR Staff OR Principal OR Manager OR Chief)
Keywords
("systems engineering" OR integration OR requirements OR "system safety" OR "MIL-STD-882") AND (vehicle OR combat OR ground OR turret OR vetronics OR C4ISR OR mission OR defense) AND (DOORS OR MBSE OR SysML OR Cameo OR verification)
Filters: Location: per req anchor (Charleston 30 mi / DFW 35 mi / Detroit 40 mi / Yuma 30 mi). Years: 7+ (Staff/Principal 10+). Industry: Defense & Space.
Run notes: Detroit's ground-vehicle corridor (GVSC/TACOM ecosystem) is the deepest pool for this family.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 300-800 combined
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "Integration Engineer" OR "Requirements Engineer" OR "Safety Engineer" OR "Vehicle Engineer")
Keywords
(requirements OR integration OR verification OR "safety case" OR hazard OR DOORS OR MBSE) AND (military OR defense OR armored OR automotive OR aerospace)
Filters: Location: widen — Detroit metro 60 mi (auto-defense crossover), Texas statewide, SC statewide, national for Yuma. Veteran filter ON (Army 91/94, USMC 21xx backgrounds).
Run notes: Auto-industry systems/safety engineers (ISO 26262) convert well to MIL-STD-882 work — Detroit's hidden feeder.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 1,500+ profiles
Title
("Systems Engineer" OR "Project Engineer" OR "Integration")
Keywords
(requirements OR integration OR "systems engineering") AND (defense OR vehicle OR platform OR DoD)
Filters: Location: United States, Open to Work + relocation. Years: 5+.
Run notes: Relocation net; Yuma reqs live here — sell proving-ground mission + Southwest cost of living.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: General Dynamics Land Systems (Sterling Heights MI)BAE Systems Platforms (Sterling Heights MI / York PA)American Rheinmetall Vehicles (Sterling Heights)Oshkosh DefenseLeonardo DRS (vetronics)GM DefenseTextron Systems
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: US Army GVSC / TACOM civilian engineers (Warren MI)Hanwha Defense USAElbit peer program staff at primesL3HarrisRaytheonGeneral Dynamics Mission SystemsAM General
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: automotive systems/safety engineers (ISO 26262 — Ford, GM, Stellantis, Bosch, ZF)Yuma Proving Ground contractor alumniBoeing SC engineers open to defense (Charleston)transitioning Army maintenance/test officers

Exclusions

Exclude current Elbit Systems of America employees; candidates already assigned to these reqs in TalentBase; pure-IT 'systems engineers'. Safety req (1487): require hazard-analysis evidence, not just the word safety.

Subjects: Platform work, proving-ground honest | Systems engineering that meets dirt | A vehicle program with room for your name
Initial InMail
{FIRST} — your platform-systems background is the reason this note exists. The retained brief is a {ROLE} in {LOC} for Elbit Systems of America: combat-vehicle and mission-systems work where the requirements you author get validated at a proving ground, not in a slide review. The safety cases are real, the integration is physical, and the feedback loop is measured in test miles. {TECHLINE} I selected your profile on three signals — systems depth, platform or vehicle context, and evidence you've carried work through verification — because that's the specific combination this program's leadership is short on. There's a dimension to the fleet this touches that I only discuss live. If building things that leave the lab appeals to you, send a current resume and name two times; I'll lay the rest out. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — briefly: the crews who ride these platforms are the mission statement. The engineers on this program say that part out loud. The door I mentioned is still open.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — the engineering meat here: hazard analysis with teeth, requirements under configuration control, and integration across hull, sensors and software where every interface has an owner. If ISO 26262 or MIL-STD-882 shaped how you think, you'd be conversant on day one. Worth a call?
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — closing gracefully. Nothing needed from you. If the season changes and platform work calls to you, I'd welcome the conversation then — and I'll flag you first when the next one opens.
Verify on first call: Verify US-person status and clearance eligibility; for the safety seat verify MIL-STD-882/hazard-analysis artifacts; for Manager/Chief verify team scale and program scope.
Flexibility: Auto-industry systems and functional-safety engineers (ISO 26262) are approved converts; level flexes for proven platform experience.

Test Engineering (Roanoke VA · Fort Worth TX)

3 requisitions · 1267, 1321, 1555
▶
Test engineering for electro-optics and guided-munitions programs — ATE, environmental test and production test on hardware that must not fail in the field.

Search Nets

Net 1 — Narrow / Precision · expect 30-120 profiles
Title
("Test Engineer" OR "Test Engineering") AND (Senior OR Principal OR Lead)
Keywords
(ATE OR "automated test" OR LabVIEW OR TestStand OR "environmental test" OR "MIL-STD-810" OR qualification) AND (defense OR aerospace OR munition OR missile OR electro-optic)
Filters: Location: per req (Roanoke 30 mi / DFW 35 mi). Years: 5+ (Principal: 10+). Industry: Defense & Space, Aviation & Aerospace.
Run notes: Precision pool; DFW is deep for munitions test.
Net 2 — Smart / Recommended · expect 200-500 profiles
Title
("Test Engineer" OR "Validation Engineer" OR "Hardware Test" OR "Integration and Test")
Keywords
(LabVIEW OR TestStand OR Python OR "test fixture" OR "test procedure" OR ESS OR HASS OR vibration OR thermal) AND (electronics OR hardware OR avionics)
Filters: Location: widen per anchor (VA statewide / TX). Years: 3+. Veteran filter on — military test/avionics backgrounds convert well.
Run notes: Core working net.
Net 3 — Wide / Market Discovery · expect 800-2,000 profiles
Title
("Test Engineer" OR "Test Technician" OR "Quality Engineer")
Keywords
(test OR ATE OR LabVIEW OR qualification) AND (defense OR aerospace OR automotive OR electronics)
Filters: Location: United States, relocation-open. Years: 3+.
Run notes: Discovery net; adjacent-industry test engineers (auto, rail, semicon) convert.

Target Companies

Tier 1 — direct competitors: Lockheed Martin (Fort Worth / Grand Prairie)Raytheon (McKinney/Tucson munitions)L3HarrisGeneral Dynamics OTSNorthrop GrummanBAE Systems (Radford VA)Textron Systems
Tier 2 — adjacent industry: NTS / Element Materials TechnologyCollins AerospaceLeonardo DRSKratosBellHoneywell Aerospace
Tier 3 — feeders & converts: NI/Emerson Test & Measurement ecosystem engineersAverna / ATS automation integratorsVolvo Trucks (Dublin VA) testWabtec (Salem VA) testmilitary ATE veterans (Navy AT, USAF 2A6)

Exclusions

Exclude pure software-QA profiles; exclude current Elbit employees; exclude candidates already assigned in TalentBase.

Subjects: The signature under 'passes test' | Test as a first-class discipline | Fixtures, chambers, consequence
Initial InMail
{FIRST} — test engineers who build the fixture, own the procedure and sign the qual are a different species from those who run someone else's scripts, and your background suggests the former. Elbit Systems of America has retained me for a {ROLE} in {LOC}: ATE, environmental and production test on defense hardware where 'passes' is a promise someone downrange gets to rely on. {TECHLINE} The selection logic behind this note is simple — hands-on fixture work, environmental exposure, evidence of ownership — and your profile carries all three. What I can't type is which programs the chamber schedule serves; it's the part that makes the seat interesting. If test as a craft — not an afterthought — is how you work, send a current resume with two windows and I'll walk you through it. — Jonah Adelman · The Staffing Specialist · retained search for Elbit Systems of America
Follow-up 1 · day 3-4
{FIRST} — mission, one line: everything this lab passes gets trusted by somebody who never met the engineer who tested it. That anonymity is the honor of the job. Happy to say more.
Follow-up 2 · day 7-8
{FIRST} — the problems here have texture: thermal profiles that expose weak design, vibration signatures that don't lie, automation that has to be more reliable than the units it tests. If building that machinery is the fun part for you, we should speak.
Follow-up 3 · day 12-14 (close)
{FIRST} — closing this out cleanly. Nothing required. Test seats recur here as programs grow; a resume on file means the next one reaches you before the job boards. Either way — respect for the discipline.
Verify on first call: Verify hands-on fixture/ATE build vs test-execution-only; clearance eligibility for munitions programs.
Flexibility: Adjacent-industry (auto/semicon) test engineers acceptable for Roanoke reqs per HM history.
